# CWYD v2 — Development Plan

**Repo**: [Azure-Samples/chat-with-your-data-solution-accelerator](https://github.com/Azure-Samples/chat-with-your-data-solution-accelerator)
**Branch**: `dev-v2`
**Last updated**: 2026-06-10 (see §0.0e — durable worklog + `bugs.md` tracking split. Rewritten lean 2026-06-04 — see [development_plan.old.md](development_plan.old.md) for the historical Phase 1–5 + Cleanup-audit batch 1/2 ledger)

> This is the **canonical, forward-looking** plan. The historical CU/Q ledger and per-phase closure trails live in [development_plan.old.md](development_plan.old.md) (frozen 2026-05-06). New debt and phase deltas land in §0.1 below.

> **Phase closure discipline** (Hard Rule #12 in [.github/copilot-instructions.md](../../.github/copilot-instructions.md)): debt items discovered while working on Phase N are appended to §0.1 — **never implemented inline**. Within a phase, tasks execute in numeric order from §4; no out-of-order pulls from later phases. The queue is cleared in a single dedicated audit turn at the end of the phase.

### 0.0c Session receipt (2026-06-08) — post-Phase-7 FE refactor + deploy work stream

Phase 7 is closed (`U-P7-AUDIT-4`). This receipt opens a new **post-Phase-7 (PP7)** work stream requested by the repo owner: relocate the frontend test tree, give the admin pages real browser URLs, deploy code-only to the existing `azd` env, and document the result. User-confirmed structural picks (Hard Rule #10): a new `v2/src/tests/` test root; add the `react-router-dom` dependency.

- **`U-PP7-RELOC`** — relocate the TypeScript/Vitest frontend test tree from `v2/src/frontend/tests/` to `v2/src/tests/frontend/` (mirror sub-tree preserved; the `@/` alias is unchanged because it still resolves to `v2/src/frontend/src/`). Supersedes [ADR 0012](adr/0012-frontend-test-folder-mirror.md) with [ADR 0020](adr/0020-frontend-tests-under-src-tests-frontend.md). Delivered as an **npm workspace** rooted at `v2/package.json` (members `src/frontend` = `cwyd-frontend`, `src/tests/frontend` = `cwyd-frontend-tests`): one `npm ci` at `v2/` hoists a single `node_modules` shared by both members (single React + `react-router-dom` instance). The test tree is its own package with its own `vitest.config.ts` (`include` scans its own tree, `setupFiles: ["./setup.tsx"]`, `@ → ../../frontend/src`), `tsconfig.json`, and `eslint.config.js`; the frontend package stays build-only (no `test` block, no `tsconfig.app.json`). The Docker build copies only `src/frontend`, so the production image never references the test tree or the workspace root. Hard Rule #11 TS file-name bullet + `v2-frontend.instructions.md` + `v2-tests.instructions.md` updated to the new path. The Python ASGI test `v2/tests/frontend/test_frontend_app.py` stays in the pytest tree — only the TS tests move.
- **`U-PP7-ROUTE`** — admin pages reachable at real URLs (`/admin/ingest`, `/admin/delete`, `/admin/config`, `/admin/prompt`) via `react-router-dom`; `frontend_app.py` gains an SPA catch-all so a deep-link refresh serves `index.html`. Replaces the `Section`-state view switch in `App.tsx` / `Header.tsx` with `<Routes>` + `<Link>`/`useNavigate`. Finalizes the admin-merge UX on top of the already-closed `#35d`.
- **`U-PP7-DEPLOY`** — code-only `azd deploy` (backend + frontend + function) to env `<AZD_ENV_NAME>` after the refactor lands and the local admin-flow test passes.
- **`U-PP7-DOCS`** — new `v2/docs/project_status.md` (whole-MVP status + non-blocking gap list) plus deploy / admin-UI / env-var docs; placeholders only (Hard Rule #18).

**`#35d` reconciliation.** `#35d` is ✅ cleared in §0.1 (2026-06-08, `U-P7-35D-AUDIT`); the §4 Phase 5 table row was stale at `⏳ in progress` and is corrected to ✅ done in this turn. The `U-PP7-ROUTE` URL-routing enhancement is **new** work, not a reopen of `#35d` — it builds on the completed Streamlit→React admin merge rather than re-doing it.

**Status (2026-06-08).** `U-PP7-RELOC` ✅ and `U-PP7-ROUTE` ✅ landed green. Verification from `v2/`: `npm test` **403 passed / 32 suites**, `npx tsc -p src/frontend` **0 errors**, `npx tsc -p src/tests/frontend` **0 errors**, `npm run lint` **0 errors / 9 advisory `react-refresh` warnings**, `npm run build` **exit 0**; the frontend SPA-fallback pytest [`v2/tests/frontend/test_frontend_app.py`](../tests/frontend/test_frontend_app.py) **4/4** (adds deep-link + missing-asset fallback cases). ### 0.0d Session receipt (2026-06-09) — Phase 8: `agent_framework` default + Foundry IQ Knowledge Base retrieval

Opens **Phase 8** (see §4 Phase 8 for the full ordered task table — the canonical resumable checklist). Direction from the repo owner across the 2026-06-09 planning turns: make `agent_framework` the **default** orchestrator, grounded by a Foundry IQ **Knowledge Base**, with the KB REST API version supplied as an **environment variable**. This is the v2, rules-compliant successor to the v1 BYOD *intent* (platform-grounded retrieval) — **not** a re-introduction of the removed Azure OpenAI `data_sources` mechanism (see the §2.1 BYOD clarifier).

Key architecture decisions captured during planning (full research trail in the session plan memory; ratified in [ADR 0021](adr/0021-agent-framework-foundry-iq-kb-default.md) + [ADR 0022](adr/0022-config-resolution-error-on-incompatible-overrides.md), both now **Accepted** — 0022 at `B5b`, 0021 at `C`):

- **Knowledge source = `searchIndex` over the existing `cwyd-index`.** The KB is a *pointer* that queries the live index, so CWYD's idempotent push-ingestion (`merge_or_upload_documents` / `ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE`) needs **no per-document reseed**. KB seed is one-time structural (create knowledge source + KB), analogous to creating the index. This is the key difference from MACAE's upload-once managed-vector-store pattern (CWYD does not use managed vector stores).
- **No custom MCP server.** The KB exposes a *managed* MCP endpoint hosted by Azure AI Search; the agent consumes it. The `mcpServer` (external-MCP) knowledge-source type is not used.
- **`langgraph` coexists, unchanged.** It reads the same index directly via `BaseSearch.search()` and is independent of the KB.
- **Knob scope relaxed.** Agentic retrieval moves away from per-request `top_k`; only `temperature` / `max_tokens` thread into the agent path (langgraph keeps its `top_k` / semantic knobs).
- **pgvector constraint.** Foundry IQ has **no** pgvector knowledge source, so `agent_framework` + KB is Azure-AI-Search-only. `pgvector` deployments must use `langgraph`; selecting `agent_framework` in pgvector mode raises a clean, reusable `ConfigResolutionError` (HTTP 409 + ERROR-level telemetry log) — never a silent fallback (ADR 0022). pgvector itself is already modern (HNSW + cosine); `pg_diskann` is an optional future upgrade, not a gap.

**KB REST API version** is pinned by the new env var `AZURE_AI_SEARCH_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_API_VERSION` (default `2025-11-01-preview`), following the existing `AZURE_*_API_VERSION` convention.

**Status (2026-06-09).** Phase 8 complete — the full `B0 → B1 → B-Spike → B2 → B3 → B4 → B5a → B5b → C` chain landed. ADRs 0021 + 0022 are **Accepted**; §2.1 clarifier + this receipt + the §4 Phase 8 task table are in place; ADR index completed (0019–0022). Task `C` flipped `OrchestratorSettings.name` from `langgraph` to `agent_framework` **after** KB retrieval was wired (`B4`) and the pgvector guardrail enforced (`B5b` — `ConfigResolutionError` / HTTP 409), so the default is never ungrounded. The dev `docker-compose.dev.yml` pins `CWYD_ORCHESTRATOR_NAME=langgraph` to keep the pgvector dev stack coherent.

### 0.0e Session receipt (2026-06-10) — durable file-based tracking (worklog + bugs registry)

Direction from the repo owner: plans, daily work, and bugs must live in **repo-tracked files**, never only in agent session memory (bug history was lost when a session's memory was cleared). Established the convention and wired it into the governance + agent layer.

- **New defect registry** [bugs.md](bugs.md) — the canonical log of every observed defect with sequential `BUG-####` ids, root cause, and fix. Seeded with `BUG-0001` + `BUG-0002` (the two `INGEST-EMBED-DOCKEY` ingestion bugs).
- **New daily worklog** under [worklog/](worklog/) — one `YYYY-MM-DD.md` per working day (plan / done / bugs / decisions / next), described by [worklog/README.md](worklog/README.md).
- **Hard Rule #19** added to [.github/copilot-instructions.md](../../.github/copilot-instructions.md) (durable file-based tracking); **Hard Rule #12** re-scoped so §0.1/§0.2 hold *phase debt and tasks* while *defects* live in `bugs.md`, with a one-line §0.1 pointer when phase-audit visibility is needed.
- **Agent guidance** updated: `cwyd-planner` persists the Work Order to the worklog; `cwyd-implementer` + `cwyd-tester` record bugs in `bugs.md` and append daily work; `cwyd-qa` recommends `bugs.md` entries (stays read-only).

The `INGEST-EMBED-DOCKEY` row below stays in §0.1 as the phase-audit pointer; full defect detail now lives in `bugs.md` (`BUG-0001` / `BUG-0002`).

### 0.0f Session receipt (2026-06-20) — frontend Vitest tree relocated to `v2/tests/frontend/` (ADR 0029)

Repo-owner decision revisiting [ADR 0020](adr/0020-frontend-tests-under-src-tests-frontend.md)'s recorded alternative #2: make the frontend test tree **symmetric** with the backend tree. The Vitest package moved `v2/src/tests/frontend/` → `v2/tests/frontend/` (matching `v2/tests/backend/`, `v2/tests/functions/`), and the Python ASGI test `test_frontend_app.py` moved to `v2/tests/frontend_app/` so each test directory is single-toolchain. There is no longer a `v2/src/tests/` directory. Ratified in [ADR 0029](adr/0029-frontend-tests-symmetric-under-tests-frontend.md), which supersedes ADR 0020 (and transitively [ADR 0012](adr/0012-frontend-test-folder-mirror.md)).

Mechanics: the `cwyd-frontend-tests` npm-workspace member path became `tests/frontend` in [v2/package.json](../package.json) (package name unchanged → `--workspace cwyd-frontend-tests` scripts unaffected); the test package's `@` alias re-pathed `../../frontend/src` → `../../src/frontend/src` (the alias *target* `v2/src/frontend/src` is unchanged, so test files need no import edits); `package-lock.json` regenerated; CI [`v2-frontend-checks.yml`](../../.github/workflows/v2-frontend-checks.yml) path filters + the `tsc -p tests/frontend` step updated; `Dockerfile.frontend` unaffected (copies only `src/frontend`). Guidance synced (Hard Rule #0): `v2-frontend.instructions.md`, `v2-tests.instructions.md` (`applyTo` drops `v2/src/tests/**`), Hard Rule #11 in `copilot-instructions.md`.

Verification: Vitest **566 passed / 44 files** from the new layout; relocated pytest `tests/frontend_app/test_frontend_app.py` **4 passed**; the relocated test tree typechecks with no test-tree errors (the `@` re-path resolves). **Pre-existing, out of scope:** `tsc -p src/frontend` + `npm run lint` are red on **app-source** files unrelated to this move (`src/frontend/src/api/streamChat.tsx` `exactOptionalPropertyTypes` TS2375 from the BUG-0067 error-body code; `CitationPanel.tsx` / `MessageList.tsx` lint) — confirmed pre-existing (typescript 5.9.3 matches HEAD; no `src/frontend/src` file was touched by the move). Tracked separately for a follow-up FE gate-green pass.

Forward-looking debt only. **Closed historical items live in [development_plan.old.md](development_plan.old.md) §0.1** (CU-001 through CU-013, CU-004a/b/c, Q1 through Q14, plus #7/#8/#35c).

Append-only during normal work; cleared in batch during the originating phase's end-of-phase audit.

> **Defects vs debt** (Hard Rule #12 + #19): this queue holds *phase debt and tasks*. Observed **defects** (broken or wrong runtime behavior) live in [bugs.md](bugs.md); a row here is only a one-line pointer to its `BUG-####` id when phase-audit visibility is needed.

After the existing `upsert_runtime_config(merged)` + `app.state.runtime_overrides = merged` write-back, the route fires `db.write_admin_audit(AdminAuditEntry(actor=user_id, action="patch_config", before=before, after=merged))`. **Best-effort policy**: the audit call is wrapped in a try/except whose body is `logger.exception("write_admin_audit failed; PATCH succeeded but audit row missing", extra={operation, actor, action})` and **does NOT re-raise** — the override is already persisted AND live-reloaded, so surfacing 500 to the operator would mislead them into retrying a PATCH that succeeded; the failure is observable in App Insights via the structured log. 422 validation failures (unknown field, wrong type) skip the audit entirely (no phantom rows for rejected PATCHes). `_fake_db` test helper extended with optional `audit` AsyncMock parameter; default `AsyncMock(return_value=None)` keeps every pre-existing PATCH test green. 4 new route tests in `tests/backend/test_admin.py`: success path locks the four forensic axes (actor `"u-1"` / action `"patch_config"` / before snapshot / after merged), first-PATCH `before is None`, no-audit-on-422, audit-failure-does-not-roll-back-PATCH (asserts 200 + caplog mentions `admin_audit` / `write_admin_audit`). Pyright `--strict` 0 errors; full suite 784/0/0 (was 780). Silent-except invariant clean (`logger.exception` body is policy-compliant per `test_no_silent_excepts`). **#35f fully closed.**) |

End-to-end probe against gpt-5 across api versions `2024-12-01-preview` / `2025-04-01-preview` / `2025-09-01-preview` with `reasoning_effort=medium` confirmed gpt-5 **never** populates `delta.reasoning_content` on the chat-completions stream surface (90 / 55 / 58 chunks observed, zero reasoning fields). The reasoning *summary* surface is only exposed through the Responses API. Refactor: `reason()` now calls `oai.responses.create(model=..., input=..., reasoning={"effort":"medium","summary":"auto"}, stream=True)` and dispatches stream events on the typed `evt.type` discriminator — `"response.reasoning_summary_text.delta"` → `OrchestratorChannel.REASONING`, `"response.output_text.delta"` → `OrchestratorChannel.ANSWER`. Other event types (created / in_progress / *.added / *.done / *.completed / content_part.*) carry no token payload and are intentionally dropped (ADR 0007 channel set stays narrow). Hard Rule #7 still enforced: dispatched on attribute access (`getattr(event, "type")`, `getattr(event, "delta")`) — no `from openai.types.responses import ...`. `_get_openai_client()` now passes `api_version=self._settings.openai.api_version` through to `AIProjectClient.get_openai_client(...)` because Foundry SDK ignores `OPENAI_API_VERSION` env var; without that, the cached client targets whatever default the SDK ships and `oai.responses.create` 404s on older Azure backends. `_OpenAIClient` Protocol gained `responses: _Responses` member with the canonical `async def create(**kwargs) -> Any` shape. `v2/.env` bumped `AZURE_OPENAI_API_VERSION` + `OPENAI_API_VERSION` from `2024-12-01-preview` → `2025-04-01-preview` (first stable preview surfacing Responses + reasoning summaries together). | FUNC-PILLAR-HEADER-LINT | 6 | **No AST invariant enforces the Pillar/Phase docstring header.** Hard Rule #3 mandates `"""\nPillar: ...\nPhase: ...\n"""` at the top of every new module under `v2/src/**`, but enforcement is doc-only — a missing header passes CI silently. Proposed: new AST guard `v2/tests/shared/test_pillar_phase_header.py` walking every `*.py` under `v2/src/` (skip `__init__.py` if empty, skip `tests/`) asserting the module docstring's first two non-empty lines match `^Pillar: (Stable Core\|Scenario Pack\|Configuration Layer\|Customization Layer)$` and `^Phase: \d+(\.\d+)?$`. Mirrors existing invariant test pattern (`test_no_silent_excepts.py`, `test_no_legacy_shared_imports.py`, `test_no_type_checking_or_future_annotations.py`). Defer to end-of-cleanup audit so the rule lands once instead of breaking every in-progress unit. **CLOSURE (FUNC-PILLAR-HEADER-LINT, 2026-05-30):** Landed `v2/tests/shared/test_pillar_phase_header.py` as the 7th AST invariant gate, mirroring `test_init_files_are_marker_only.py` / `test_imports_at_top_only.py` shape (`_V2_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2]`, `_SCAN_ROOTS = ("src",)`, `_EXEMPTIONS: frozenset[Path] = frozenset()` zero-carve-out, `rglob("*.py")` + skip-set `{__pycache__, .venv, build}`, per-file parametrise with `ids=lambda p: str(p.relative_to(_V2_ROOT))`). Two regex assertions per file: `_PILLAR_RE = re.compile(r"^Pillar: (Stable Core\|Scenario Pack\|Configuration Layer\|Customization Layer)$", re.MULTILINE)` and `_PHASE_RE = re.compile(r"^Phase: \d+(\.\d+)?( \([^)]+\))?$", re.MULTILINE)` — the optional `( \([^)]+\))?` parenthetical tail honours Hard Rule #16(a) carve-out (phase headers may carry the phase's standing descriptive name, e.g. `Phase: 6 (Functions blueprints / modular RAG indexing pipeline)`, but not process narrative — that is policed separately by `test_no_process_narrative_in_src.py`). Sanity guard `test_scan_actually_walked_files` asserts `len(_ALL_FILES) >= 90` to prevent silent zero-case regression. | IA-C1 | 6 (debt) | **AST gate codifies Hard Rule #13; B7 back-fix lands in same turn (user-approved Option B).** New `v2/tests/shared/test_init_files_are_marker_only.py` walks every `__init__.py` under `v2/src/` + `v2/tests/` (24 files at audit close), parses each with `ast.parse`, and asserts the top-level body is either empty or a single `ast.Expr(value=ast.Constant(value=str))` docstring node. | U8d | 6 | **First concrete parser landed: `TextParser` (`"txt"` key) in `backend/core/providers/parsers/text.py`** — fourth unit of Phase 6 task #41, resumes the parsing tier after the IA-Bx detour. Self-registers via `@registry.register("txt")` against the `parsers` `Registry[type[BaseParser]]` declared in `parsers/registry.py`; eager side-effect import `from . import text` added at the bottom of `parsers/registry.py` (per Hard Rule #13 Option SE-1) so the registration fires at process start without `__init__.py` doing any work. Eager import suppressed with both `# noqa: E402, F401` (ruff/flake8) AND `# pyright: ignore[reportUnusedImport]` because pyright doesn't honor the flake8 directive — the side-effect-import pattern is unavoidable for plug-and-play registration and is now mechanically warning-free across both linters. **Chunking strategy** = paragraph-based, blank-line separated via `re.compile(r"(?:\r?\n[ \t]*){2,}")` (handles `\r\n` line endings + intermediate whitespace lines). v2 removed the chunker primitive (decision D2 in §4.6.1) — each parser owns the format-appropriate split. For plain text, paragraphs are the natural semantic unit, match v1's default chunking, surface cleanly in downstream embedders, and keep `Chunk.id = f"{source}__{index}"` deterministic so re-ingest produces stable Search keys. Per-paragraph whitespace stripped; whitespace-only / empty input returns `[]` so the embedder + indexer never see zero-content chunks. **UTF-8 decoded with `errors="strict"`** — malformed bytes propagate as `UnicodeDecodeError` to the Functions queue-trigger runtime, engaging retry → poison-queue (preferred over silent `errors="replace"` which would mask producer-side corruption — matches the U8b `AzureError` re-raise philosophy). Hard Rule #11 honored: no `TYPE_CHECKING`, no `__future__`; all annotations resolve at class-definition time. Pillar = Stable Core. **Test count 1008 → 1025** (+12 net-new U8d tests: registered-under-txt / is-baseparser-subclass / registry-get-constructs-instance / single-paragraph-yields-single-chunk / blank-line-splits-into-two-with-sequential-indices / multiple-blank-lines-collapse / per-paragraph-whitespace-stripped / empty-bytes-returns-empty-list / whitespace-only-returns-empty-list / non-utf8-raises-UnicodeDecodeError / source-propagates-into-every-chunk / returned-chunks-are-frozen; +5 deltas from prior unrelated work since IA-D1's snapshot). `pyright src/backend src/functions` → 0/0/0. **Pre-existing 4 starlette `HTTP_422_UNPROCESSABLE_ENTITY` `DeprecationWarning`s** in `tests/backend/test_admin.py` persist (4 warnings in pytest output, unchanged by U8d) — separate concern queued under `BACKEND-422-DEPRECATION-WARN` debt below. | `v2/src/backend/core/providers/parsers/text.py` (new), `v2/src/backend/core/providers/parsers/registry.py` (eager `from . import text` added with dual lint suppression), `v2/tests/backend/core/providers/parsers/test_text_parser.py` (new) | Phase 6 (this row) | ✅ cleared (2026-05-26) |
| U8i-SCOPE-FIX | 6 | **Step-0 sync (Hard Rule #0) — §4.6.1 U8i wrapper corrected.** Original U8i row specified `@map_function_exceptions("batch_push", trigger="queue")` but that decorator is typed `Callable[_P, Awaitable[func.HttpResponse]]` and emits 422/502/500 JSON — wrong contract for a queue trigger, which must return `None` and re-raise so the Functions runtime's retry → poison-queue policy engages (the exact behavior every `batch_push/*` module docstring already commits to). Reusing it on the queue trigger would *swallow* exceptions and return `HttpResponse(502)`, which the runtime treats as success → message permanently deleted instead of retried/poisoned = silent data loss. Cleanest fix per "clean, modular, easy to scale" (user pick 2026-05-26): new sibling decorator `log_queue_errors(operation: str)` in the same `functions/core/exception_mapping.py` module — one decorator per trigger kind, both with the same `operation`/`trigger` log-tag shape, scales to any future queue/event-grid/timer trigger. Scope correction lands as a new **U7i** row inserted between U8h and U8i (numbered U7i because the unit extends the U7c–U7h `functions/core/` substrate, not the `batch_push` blueprint specifically); U8i row updated to `@log_queue_errors("batch_push")` + dep `U7i`; U8j blueprint registration unchanged. Locked sub-decisions: (D1) decorator name = `log_queue_errors` (accurate verb — no wire mapping, just structured log + reraise; alternatives `map_queue_exceptions` / `observe_queue_errors` rejected); (D2) same module, not a new file (siblings, per FastAPI router-grouping precedent); (D3) `ValidationError` branch logs **warning** (caller error), `AzureError` + generic `Exception` branches log **exception** (server-side fault) — matches HTTP decorator + [v2/docs/exception_handling_policy.md] convention; (D4) all branches **re-raise** (decorator is observability-only; runtime owns retry → poison); (D5) `ValidationError` deterministic-failure burn (5 retries × ~1s each per envelope drift) accepted as cost of staying inside Functions Python's built-in retry policy — revisit only with measured hot bug pathway (custom poison-queue output binding rejected as scope creep). **Pillar = Stable Core** (decorator + blueprint both extend the existing `functions/core/` plug-point). **No code touched in this Step-0 row** — implementation lands in U7i (next turn) + U8i (turn after) + U8j (turn after that). | `v2/docs/development_plan.md` (this ledger row + §4.6.1 row update — `+U7i` row, `U8i` decorator rename) | Phase 6 (this row, doc-only) | ✅ cleared (2026-05-26) |
| U8i-EMBEDDER-CTOR-DEBT | 6 (debt) | **`BaseEmbedder` does not declare a construction contract or lifecycle.** Surfaced while shipping U8i (`batch_push/blueprint.py`) — the first place in v2 that constructs an embedder through `embedders_registry.registry.get("azure_openai")`. `BaseEmbedder` (`v2/src/backend/core/providers/embedders/base.py`) currently declares only `async def embed(...)`; the concrete `AzureOpenAIEmbedder` adds `__init__(settings, credential, *, llm_provider=None)` + `async def aclose()`. The registry stores `type[BaseEmbedder]`, so pyright `--strict` rejects both the `(settings=..., credential=...)` call and the `aclose()` read at the blueprint call site. Two clean fixes — (a) tighten `BaseEmbedder` with an abstract `__init__(settings, credential)` + abstract `aclose()` so the registry's typed value reflects what every concrete embedder must support, or (b) define a `SupportsEmbedderConstruction` Protocol in `embedders/registry.py` and widen the registry generic to it. Both are structural (Hard Rule #10 — needs user confirmation); both are deferred to a dedicated post-Phase-6 turn because Phase 6 already has its own §4.6.1 task ordering and Hard Rule #12 forbids mid-phase backfills. **Workaround at the U8i call site:** explicit `# pyright: ignore[reportCallIssue]` on the `embedder_cls(settings=..., credential=...)` line + `# pyright: ignore[reportAttributeAccessIssue]` on the `await embedder.aclose()` line, both annotated with a comment referencing this ledger ID. Runtime behavior is correct (the only registered concrete IS `AzureOpenAIEmbedder`, which accepts those kwargs + exposes `aclose`); the ignore is a typing escape valve, not a behavioral risk. **No code touched in this Step-0 row** beyond the two `# pyright: ignore` annotations + comments already shipped in U8i. **Cleared when:** a second concrete embedder lands (forces the construction contract decision) OR a Stable Core hardening turn formalizes `BaseEmbedder.__init__` + `aclose()`, whichever comes first. **CLOSURE (2026-05-28):** user picked Option (b) Protocol (Hard Rule #10 structural approval). Two clean fixes — (a) drop the `*` from the Protocol so any positional-or-keyword signature satisfies it (preserves the spirit of "keyword-only at the call site is convention, not contract") — possibly add a comment that the production call sites still use keyword form; or (b) introduce a thin `SearchWriterAdapter` class in `search/writer.py` that wraps `SearchClient` and exposes the keyword-only signature, then construct that adapter at the blueprint call site instead of casting. | ENUM-OPTIONAL-DEFER | 6 (decision) | **P2 — decision marker: `db_type` / `index_store` / `OrchestratorSettings.name` / `DeploymentAttr` STAY as `Literal[...]` per Hard Rule #11 carve-out.** Audit batch (2026-05-26) inventoried four additional `Literal[...]` declarations and confirmed each is a Pydantic-model **type annotation** only (not runtime dispatch): `db_type: Literal["cosmosdb","postgres"]` on `DatabaseSettings`, `index_store: Literal["azure_search","pgvector"]` on `SearchSettings`, `OrchestratorSettings.name: Literal["langgraph","agent_framework"]`, and the `DeploymentAttr` Literal on `LLMDeployment`. These literals are consumed by `*_registry.registry.get(settings.<field>)` — the registry lookup uses the string as a dict key, not as a dispatch comparison; the registry returns the registered provider class regardless of which literal was matched. **No migration required.** Recording this decision here so the question doesn't keep getting re-opened in subsequent audits. **Cleared by decision (no code change).** **Re-open trigger:** if any of these four fields gains a runtime equality comparison (`if settings.<field> == "..."`), the carve-out no longer applies and a new enum row must be queued. | n/a (decision marker — no files to touch) | Cleared by decision (2026-05-26) | ✅ closed (decision) |
| RULE15-CODIFY-BACKFILL | 6 (Standards turn) | **Hard Rule #15 codified + AST gate landed + 7 production back-fill sites refactored, in a single Standards turn between U10a and U10b (Hard Rule #12 mid-phase exception, user-approved this turn).** User flagged the pattern `return {"id": chunk.id, "content": chunk.content, "title": chunk.source, "content_vector": vector, ...} -> dict[str, object]` as "should be an specific class/model" and asked to (a) codify the rule, (b) inventory every offender, (c) back-fill them — explicitly approving the mid-phase audit ("let stop here and add this to our rules and do a refactory" + "Start implementation" after plan presentation). Per Hard Rule #12 the "current task literally cannot proceed without the missed item" exception applies: U10b's `search_skill` handler is about to author a new Functions-pipeline return shape (per-record output payloads), so codifying the typed-model rule now prevents U10b from emitting fresh `dict[str, object]` debt that would be immediately back-filled. **(A) Rule codification.** New Hard Rule #15 inserted into `.github/copilot-instructions.md` verbatim between #14 and the "## Workflow contract" heading: closed-set dict returns must be typed Pydantic `BaseModel` (frozen, `extra="forbid"`), `model_dump()` is the SDK boundary, arity 1 still earns a model (the "one field doesn't need a model" door always becomes "two fields don't either"), four boundary carve-outs spelled out — (a) third-party SDK responses (`dict[str, Any]` from `asyncpg`/`cosmos`/`azure_search`), (b) externally-defined protocol payloads (Easy Auth principal claims blob, JWT payloads), (c) stdlib/SDK structural arguments typed `Mapping[str, object]` (`logger.<level>(extra=...)`, `func.HttpResponse(headers=...)`) when callers spread with `**` to merge ad-hoc per-call fields, (d) test capture buffers (`captured: dict[str, object] = {}` accumulators in test stubs). Cross-reference appended to Hard Rule #11's Python sub-bullet so the two type-discipline rules read together: #11 governs *closed-set string literals* (use `StrEnum`) + *internal plumbing* (no `Any`); #15 governs *closed-set dict returns* (use a `BaseModel`); same boundary carve-outs apply to both. **(B) AST gate.** New `v2/tests/shared/test_no_anonymous_dict_returns.py` (~250 LOC) walks every `*.py` under `v2/src/` (excluding `__pycache__`, `.venv`), parses each with `ast.parse`, and on each `FunctionDef` whose `.returns` annotation matches `dict[str, ...]` / `Mapping[str, ...]` / `list[dict[str, ...]]` / `Optional[...]` / PEP 604 union variants raises a parametrised failure naming the file + function qualname. Allow-list as `frozenset[tuple[str, str]]` of `(module_dotted_path, function_qualname)` tuples, each with a one-line justification comment in the module docstring: `("backend.app", "_request_extras")` (logger.warning structural extras — Rule 15(c)), `("backend.dependencies", "_decode_easy_auth_principal")` (Easy Auth principal claims blob — Rule 15(b)), `("backend.core.providers.databases.cosmosdb", "CosmosDBClient._read_item")` (asyncpg-style raw row from Cosmos SDK — Rule 15(a)), `("backend.core.providers.llm.foundry_iq", "FoundryIQ._to_openai_messages")` (openai ChatCompletionMessageParam TypedDict via `model_dump(exclude_none=True)` — Rule 15(a)+(b) — IS the model→wire boundary the rule prescribes, not a violation). Mirrors `test_init_files_are_marker_only.py` shape: `pytest.parametrize` with `ids=lambda` for clean failure messages; companion `test_allow_list_entries_resolve_to_real_functions` guards against allow-list drift (every entry must resolve via `importlib.import_module` + `getattr` chain); companion `test_scan_actually_walked_files` guards against silent zero-case regression. **(C) Production back-fill — 7 sites identified by the gate, 2 expanded via blueprint pass-through detection.** **(C.1) `backend/core/types.py`:** new `SearchDocument(BaseModel)` model sibling of `SearchResult` (`model_config = ConfigDict(frozen=True, extra="forbid")`; fields `id: str`, `content: str`, `title: str = ""`, `content_vector: list[float] = Field(default_factory=list[float])`). Docstring cites Rule #15 + the read-side mirror at `backend.core.providers.search.azure_search.AzureSearch._to_result` + `_DEFAULT_SELECT_FIELDS = ("id", "content", "title", "url")` so read/write stay in lockstep on any future schema upgrade; YAGNI breadcrumb explicitly omits `url` field until `batch_push`/`add_url` produce a SAS or source URL (when that arrives, add to model AND `_DEFAULT_SELECT_FIELDS` AND `SearchResult` together). Added to `__all__`. **(C.2) `backend/core/providers/search/writer.py`:** `push_documents(search_client, docs: Sequence[SearchDocument]) -> list[Any]` (was `Sequence[Mapping[str, Any]]`); body now `payload = [d.model_dump() for d in docs]` — single `model_dump()` call IS the SDK boundary; `SupportsMergeOrUploadDocuments` Protocol UNCHANGED (Azure SDK contract — still `Sequence[Mapping[str, Any]]` per Rule 15(a) boundary carve-out; Protocol docstring spells out the deliberate boundary). **(C.3) `functions/function_app.py`:** new inline `HealthPayload(BaseModel)` (`frozen=True`, `extra="forbid"`, `status: str = "ok"`) with docstring explicitly citing Rule #15's "arity 1 still earns a model" carve-out reasoning; `_health_payload() -> HealthPayload`; route body switched from `json.dumps(_health_payload())` → `_health_payload().model_dump_json()` (drops `import json` from production module). **(C.4) `functions/add_url/handler.py`:** `_build_document(chunk, vector) -> SearchDocument` + `add_url_handler(...) -> list[SearchDocument]`. Body returns `SearchDocument(id=chunk.id, content=chunk.content, title=chunk.source, content_vector=vector)`. **(C.5) `functions/batch_push/handler.py`:** same pattern as C.4 — duplicated intentionally per blueprint independence (no `_shared/` package per `FUNC-SHARED-PKG` row above; cross-blueprint types live under `functions/core/` only when ≥2 blueprints share an identical contract — `SearchDocument` lives in `backend/core/types.py` because both backend search-writer + Functions ingestion handlers consume it). **(C.6) `functions/add_url/blueprint.py::_execute`** + **(C.7) `functions/batch_push/blueprint.py::_execute`:** both `_execute(request|message, settings) -> list[SearchDocument]` (was `list[dict[str, object]]`). Pure pass-through dispatchers — caller `add_url`/`batch_push` reads `len(documents)` only, no shape dependency. **(D) Test back-fill — 7 test files updated.** `v2/tests/backend/core/test_types.py` +4 sibling test functions (`test_search_document_is_frozen_and_forbids_extras` / `test_search_document_round_trips_via_model_dump` / `test_search_document_defaults_match_read_side_optional_fields` / `test_search_document_is_in_module_exports`) mirroring the `RuntimeConfig` `__all__` membership pattern. `v2/tests/functions/test_function_app.py` +1 frozen-and-forbid-extras test; existing `_health_payload() == {"status": "ok"}` line flipped to `== HealthPayload()` + a `model_dump()` round-trip assertion. `v2/tests/backend/core/providers/search/test_writer.py` raw dict literals replaced with `SearchDocument(...)` instances; SDK call assertion switched to `documents=[d.model_dump() for d in docs]`. `v2/tests/functions/add_url/test_handler.py` + `v2/tests/functions/batch_push/test_handler.py` `expected docs` literals flipped to `SearchDocument(...)` lists; writer-call assertion flipped to `model_dump()` form. `v2/tests/functions/add_url/test_blueprint.py` + `v2/tests/functions/batch_push/test_blueprint.py` `Callable[..., Awaitable[list[dict[str, object]]]]` signatures + all `fake_execute` return annotations flipped to `list[SearchDocument]`; `expected_docs` literal + the inline batch_push fake-handler list literal flipped to `SearchDocument(...)`. `captured: dict[str, object] = {}` at `test_blueprint.py:115` left untouched (Rule 15(d) test capture buffer carve-out). **(E) Verification.** Gate: `pytest tests/shared/test_no_anonymous_dict_returns.py` → 2 passed + 1 skipped (zero offenders post-refactor; sanity tests green). | U11.5-INLINE-TASK-NUM-SWEEP | 6 (debt) | **Inline `task #N` cross-references remain in production docstrings across v2/src/.** Surfaced during U11.5's Hard Rule #16 codification + scrub turn. Per Hard Rule #16 carve-out (a) the **Phase header tails** carrying `, task #N` were stripped during the U11.5 scrub (every Phase header now carries only the phase's standing descriptive name); the remaining `task #N` references are **inline** narrative pointers (typically `(Phase 6 task #41)` or `per Phase 6 task #43`) inside body paragraphs of provider/orchestrator/types/settings docstrings under `v2/src/backend/` + `v2/src/functions/`. | B-IMPL-FACTORY-CACHE | 3 (debt) | **`AgentFrameworkOrchestrator` constructs a fresh `FoundryAgent` per request via `_default_agent_factory(project_endpoint=..., agent_name=..., credential=...)`.** Surfaced during B-IMPL Unit 2 implementation (2026-06-01) and confirmed during the Unit 6 audit (2026-06-02). The OSS `agent_framework_foundry.FoundryAgent` constructor opens an HTTP session against the Foundry project endpoint on each instantiation; under per-request orchestrator construction this is one new session per conversation turn. Workaround in U2: the class accepts an injected `agent_factory` callable (test seam) and falls back to `_default_agent_factory` in production; this works correctly but leaves a per-turn allocation wart. **Fix scope (single hardening unit, post-Phase-7 backend tier):** cache `FoundryAgent` instances per `(project_endpoint, agent_name, credential_identity)` tuple at the orchestrator-registry layer (likely a module-level `dict` keyed by the tuple, populated lazily, drained at lifespan shutdown via a new `shutdown_orchestrator_agents()` hook). Trade-off to weigh during implementation: caching across requests requires that `FoundryAgent` be thread-safe / re-entrant under concurrent `agent.run(messages, stream=True)` calls — verify against the OSS SDK docs before committing to a shared instance; if not re-entrant, fall back to a connection-pool-style `asyncio.Queue` of pre-constructed agents instead. **Cleared when:** the cache lands behind a tested hook OR the OSS SDK documents per-call construction as the intended pattern. Not blocking any other work. | BICEP-COSMOS-PUBLIC-ACCESS-INCONSISTENCY | 7 (debt — surfaced during first cloud smoke 2026-06-08) | **`v2/infra/main.bicep` ships Cosmos with `publicNetworkAccess: Disabled` while Search / OpenAI / Foundry (`aisa-*`) all ship `Enabled`, and the Container Apps Environment has no VNet integration (`properties.vnetConfiguration: null`).** Backend ACA replica's public egress IP is blocked by the Cosmos firewall — the `_lifespan` `await database_client.get_runtime_config()` call (`v2/src/backend/app.py:125` → `cosmosdb.py:518` `container.read_item(...)`) raises `CosmosHttpResponseError: (Forbidden) Request originated from IP <staticIp> through public internet. This is blocked by your Cosmos DB account firewall settings`; FastAPI lifespan fails, every replica goes `ActivationFailed`, no rev ever serves traffic. Runtime unblocker shipped 2026-06-08: `az cosmosdb update -g <RG> -n cosmos-<DATA_SUFFIX> --public-network-access Enabled` then force a new rev via `az containerapp update --set-env-vars BOOT_NONCE=<ts>` (a `revision restart` does NOT unstick an `ActivationFailed` rev — must create rev N+1). **Fix:** Bicep audit must either (a) flip the Cosmos module to `publicNetworkAccess: 'Enabled'` for parity with the other three data-plane services (smallest blast radius, matches today's runtime fix, keeps the all-public posture consistent), OR (b) add private endpoints + DNS zones + ACA `vnetConfiguration` (workloadProfile name + subnet ids for `infrastructureSubnetId` + `internal: true`) for **all four** services together so the posture stays uniform (larger blast radius, requires `Microsoft.App/managedEnvironments` recreation since VNet config is immutable post-create). Today's drift is the **inconsistency**, not the choice between the two postures — pick one and apply to all four. | `v2/infra/main.bicep` (Cosmos module + AVM search / cognitiveservices modules + ACA env module), `v2/infra/modules/**` | Phase 7 audit / next infra hardening turn | ✅ cleared (2026-06-08, C1) — added `networkAclBypass: 'None'` to the Cosmos `networkRestrictions` block in `v2/infra/main.bicep:1243` to match MACAE's reference shape (`{ networkAclBypass, publicNetworkAccess }`). AVM `document-db/database-account:0.19.0` already defaults the bypass to `'None'` (per its template `coalesce(...,'None')`), so this is a posture-explicit no-op on deployed state — the structural intent now matches MACAE rather than relying on AVM defaults. The four data-plane services (Cosmos / Search / OpenAI / Foundry) all use the same `enablePrivateNetworking ? 'Disabled' : 'Enabled'` ternary at `main.bicep:505/735/810/873/1245`; with `enablePrivateNetworking=false` (default) all four bicep-declare `'Enabled'`. The runtime drift the smoke uncovered was unsticked via `az cosmosdb update --public-network-access Enabled` + force a new ACA rev; if the same drift re-appears on the next `azd up`, escalate as a separate AVM-behavior debt (not a bicep-config debt). Private-endpoints + ACA `vnetConfiguration` posture (debt option b) remains an option for a later infra-hardening turn but is intentionally NOT taken today — the user picked posture (a) MACAE-aligned shape. |
| DOCKERFILE-BACKEND-RELOAD-DEV-FLAG | 7 (debt — surfaced during first cloud smoke 2026-06-08) | **`v2/docker/Dockerfile.backend` CMD ships uvicorn with `--reload` (dev-only WatchFiles flag) in the image deployed to Container Apps.** Visible in the rev 7 console logs (`INFO: Will watch for changes in these directories: ['/app']` + `INFO: Started reloader process [1] using WatchFiles`). The image is single-stage and double-duty as the dev image (`docker compose -f v2/docker/docker-compose.dev.yml`) and the deployed image (`az acr build` + `azd deploy`), so the `--reload` flag bleeds into production. WatchFiles + `--reload` adds (a) startup latency from filesystem scanning, (b) memory overhead from the reloader supervisor + worker, (c) risk that a transient filesystem touch (e.g. a log rotation, a tmpfile write) restarts the worker mid-request, (d) a confusing process tree (reloader PID 1 + worker PID 8 in the logs). **Fix:** split into a dev `CMD` (current `--reload`) and a prod `CMD` (`uvicorn backend.app:app --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000 --app-dir /app/src` with NO `--reload` and NO `--workers >1` — lifespan singletons aren't safe for multi-worker today; gunicorn / multi-worker would need explicit per-process lifespan audit). Options: (a) multi-stage Dockerfile with a `dev` target and a `prod` target; (b) two Dockerfiles `Dockerfile.backend.dev` + `Dockerfile.backend`; (c) single Dockerfile + `ENV CWYD_UVICORN_RELOAD=` conditional in CMD entrypoint script; (d) `azd`/`acr build` passes `--target prod` to a multi-stage build. (a) or (d) preferred — keeps the dev experience single-command (`docker compose ... up` defaults to dev target) and makes the prod artifact explicit. | `v2/docker/Dockerfile.backend`, `v2/docker/docker-compose.dev.yml`, `v2/azure.yaml` (docker target hint), `v2/scripts/azd-deploy.ps1` (if any), `azd hooks` | Phase 7 audit / next infra hardening turn | ✅ cleared (2026-06-08, C2) — MACAE-pattern single image (per user direction "we don't do prod, check what we do multi-agent"). `v2/docker/Dockerfile.backend` CMD drops `--reload` and ships a deploy-ready entrypoint; `v2/docker/docker-compose.dev.yml` `backend` service adds a `command:` override that re-injects `uvicorn ... --reload --app-dir /app/src` so the dev compose stack keeps hot-reload while azd deploy ships the unchanged image. No multi-stage, no `target:` hint in `v2/azure.yaml`, no entrypoint shim. Header comment in `Dockerfile.backend` updated from "Backend dev image" → "Backend image — FastAPI + uv (shared by docker-compose.dev + azd deploy)". | INGEST-EMBED-DOCKEY | 6 (debt — single back-fill during local end-to-end smoke 2026-06-10) | **Two ingestion bugs blocked the `batch_push` pipeline from producing any indexed document end-to-end; both fixed test-first this turn.** Hard Rule #12 single-back-fill justification: the active Phase 6 ingestion task literally could not index a chunk without them (embed returned `404`, then Search push returned `InvalidDocumentKey`), so the fixes landed inline rather than queued. **(a) Embeddings routed to the project endpoint + missing `dimensions`.** `FoundryIQ.embed()` reused the project-scoped OpenAI client (correct for chat / agents) for embeddings; the Foundry **project** route exposes no `embeddings` path → `404`. It also never passed `dimensions`, so a `text-embedding-3-large` deployment would emit 3072-dim vectors against the 1536-dim `content_vector` index field. **Fix:** new `FoundryIQ._get_embeddings_client()` targets the **account** endpoint (`AZURE_AI_SERVICES_ENDPOINT` + `/openai/v1`); `embed()` passes `dimensions=settings.openai.embedding_dimensions`. **(b) Invalid Azure Search document key.** Parsers minted `Chunk.id = f"{source}__{index}"`; when `source` is a filename, its extension dot makes the key illegal (Azure Search keys allow only letters / digits / `_` / `-` / `=`). **Fix:** new Stable-Core `BaseParser.make_chunk_id(source, index)` SHA-256-hashes the readable `f"{source}__{index}"` into a key-safe hex digest (mirrors v1 `source_document.py` `hashlib` precedent); both parsers call it; the readable name survives on `Chunk.source` / Search `title`; read-side `_to_result` already treats `id` as opaque. **Test-gap root cause (why neither was caught):** `test_foundry_iq.py` fully mocks the OpenAI client (hiding project-vs-account routing) and the parser tests asserted the raw `id` literal (baking in the bad key charset). New `test_base.py` (5 tests) asserts key-safety via a charset regex against the helper contract, not a magic string. **Verified live:** local func host + cloud Cosmos / Search / Foundry — `batch_start` enqueued 2 PDFs → both `batch_push` Succeeded → `cwyd-index` doc count `0 → 15`. **Open sub-observation (separate candidate row):** `batch_push` logs `aiohttp` `Unclosed client session` / `Unclosed connector` from the `AzureSearch` write client — the SDK session is not awaited-closed on the write path (non-failing resource-leak hygiene; cleanup-path obligation per Hard Rule #14). | `v2/src/backend/core/providers/llm/foundry_iq.py`, `v2/src/backend/core/providers/parsers/base.py`, `v2/src/functions/core/parsers/{text_parser,document_intelligence_parser}.py`, `v2/src/backend/core/types.py`, `v2/tests/backend/core/providers/parsers/test_base.py`, `v2/tests/functions/core/parsers/test_{text_parser,document_intelligence_parser}.py`, `v2/tests/backend/core/providers/llm/test_foundry_iq.py` | 2026-06-10 (this turn) | ✅ cleared — both fixes verified live end-to-end (15 docs indexed); `Unclosed client session` sub-observation remains ☐ open as an AzureSearch write-path cleanup item |

Every frontend image in `cr<SUFFIX>` carries a manual `cwyd-<date>-<sha>` tag, never an `azd-deploy-*` tag — confirming `azd deploy` has never built/pushed this container (the backend, on `host: containerapp`, builds + pushes correctly). The earlier "frontend shell 200 / SPA HTML" smoke row was a **false positive** — the placeholder page also returns `200` + HTML, so a status-only probe cannot tell it apart from the real SPA. **Cleared by hand this turn:** (1) `az acr build -r cr<SUFFIX> -t chat-with-your-data-v2/frontend-<AZD_ENV_NAME>:cwyd-<date>-<sha> -t ...:latest -f docker/Dockerfile.frontend --target prod --build-arg VITE_BACKEND_URL=<AZURE_BACKEND_URL> .` (`vite build` → `dist/`, image pushed); (2) `az webapp config container set -g <RESOURCE_GROUP> -n app-frontend-<SUFFIX> --container-image-name cr<SUFFIX>.azurecr.io/...:cwyd-<date>-<sha> --container-registry-url https://cr<SUFFIX>.azurecr.io`; (3) `az resource update --ids <appId>/config/web --set properties.acrUseManagedIdentityCreds=true properties.acrUserManagedIdentityID=<AZURE_UAMI_CLIENT_ID>` (the system-assigned identity lacks `AcrPull`; the UAMI holds it); (4) `WEBSITES_PORT=80` + `az webapp restart`. Verified live: root serves the real SPA (`<title>CWYD v2</title>`, `/assets/index-*.js`, no placeholder text), JS bundle `200`, baked backend URL present in the bundle. **Recurs on every `azd deploy frontend`** (azd re-zips; the manual container pointer is overwritten). **Fix scope (structural — Hard Rule #10 ask required before edit):** decide between (a) move the frontend to `host: containerapp` (mirrors the working backend deploy path), (b) add an azd `postdeploy` / custom hook that runs the `az acr build` + `az webapp config container set`, or (c) correct the `host: appservice` + `docker` container-deploy wiring so azd builds/pushes. Pair with the two ACR-pull rows in the same infra-hardening turn; also harden the deploy smoke probe to assert SPA-specific content, not just `200`. | `v2/azure.yaml` (`frontend` service), `v2/docker/Dockerfile.frontend`, `v2/infra/main.bicep` (frontend App Service module), cross-ref `ACR-AAD-AS-ARM-BICEP-DEBT` + `BACKEND-CA-ACR-REGISTRIES-BICEP-DEBT` | next infra hardening turn | ☐ open |

| ACR-AAD-AS-ARM-BICEP-DEBT | 7 (debt — surfaced 2026-06-08) | **`v2/infra/modules/container_registry.bicep` does not enable `azureAdAuthenticationAsArmPolicy`; managed-identity ACR pull from App Service silently fails with `ACRTokenRetrievalFailure -- Unauthorized` even when AcrPull RBAC is correctly assigned.** Surfaced 2026-06-08 while deploying the pinned-tag frontend image (`cwyd-202606081929-9e18f45`) to `app-frontend-<SUFFIX>`. Both UAMI and SMI held `AcrPull` on `cr<SUFFIX>` (verified via `az role assignment list --scope <acr-id>`); App Service site config carried `acrUseManagedIdentityCreds=true` with the correct `acrUserManagedIdentityID=<AZURE_UAMI_CLIENT_ID>`; manual `docker pull` from the operator's identity succeeded; yet every container start cycled `Pulling image -> ImagePullFailure -> ACRTokenRetrievalFailure -- Status Code:Unauthorized`. **Root cause:** Basic SKU ACRs ship with `policies.azureAdAuthenticationAsArmPolicy.status = "disabled"` by default. App Service exchanges the MI's AAD token for an ACR refresh token via the ARM-fronted `/azurecr.io/oauth2/exchange` path; that exchange is gated by this policy. Cross-reference fix already documented in `v2/docs/cloud_deployment.md` §3.3.2 + troubleshooting table row for `ACRTokenRetrievalFailure`. **Cleared when:** the Bicep change lands + a fresh `azd provision` on a clean RG verifies the policy is enabled post-provision. | `v2/infra/modules/container_registry.bicep` (or AVM call site) | dedicated Bicep hardening turn | ☐ open |

Legend: ☐ open · ⏳ in progress · ⏭ next · ⏸ blocked · ✅ cleared (date)

---

## 1. Architecture goals

The v2 architecture rests on three invariants:

1. **Pillars** ([pillars_of_development.md](pillars_of_development.md)) — every new core element declares one of: Stable Core, Scenario Pack, Configuration Layer, Customization Layer. Read-only product policy; never edited by agents.
2. **Plug-and-play via registry** — all swappable concerns (credentials, llm, embedders, parsers, search, chat_history, orchestrators) live under `v2/src/backend/core/providers/<domain>/` and self-register via `@registry.register("key")`. Caller code does `domain.create(key, ...)` — never `if/elif` provider dispatch (Hard Rule #4).
3. **Standalone backend, optional functions** (new in Phase 5.5) — backend runs end-to-end (chat + history + admin) without the functions container. Functions is opt-in: it ships only when the operator wants to upload + index their own files. **No code is duplicated**: anything used by both lives in `backend/core/`; functions extends via `functions/core/` (subclass / extension module that imports the base from `backend.core`).

Fourth supporting invariant — **runtime types always available** (Hard Rule #11 sub-rule, ratified 2026-05-05 in CU-013): no `if TYPE_CHECKING:`, no `from __future__ import annotations`. Genuine circular imports get fixed by extracting the shared type to a leaf module (Hard Rule #10 — ask first). Enforced by AST invariant `v2/tests/shared/test_no_type_checking_or_future_annotations.py` (a follow-up turn will move this file to `v2/tests/backend/core/_invariants/` to colocate with the source under test — pending user approval per Hard Rule #10).

---

## 2. What changes from v1 to v2

### 2.1 Removals

These are **binding** (Hard Rule #7). Never re-introduce.

| Component | Reason |
|-----------|--------|
| **One-click "Deploy to Azure" button** | Simplify to `azd`-only; ARM template maintenance overhead |
| **Poetry references** | Fully standardized on `uv`; remove any lingering Poetry config |
| **Prompt Flow orchestrator** | Replaced by Agent Framework; drops Azure ML dependency |
| **Semantic Kernel orchestrator** | Consolidate to fewer, more strategic orchestrators |
| **Streamlit admin app** | Admin features merged into the React/Vite frontend (Phase 5) |
| **Direct Azure OpenAI SDK** | Replaced by Foundry IQ for knowledge base, embeddings, chat, reasoning |
| **Azure Bot Service / Teams extension** | Deferred to a future version |
| **Key Vault for app secrets** | Replaced by RBAC + UAMI + direct env vars (MACAE pattern) |
| **BYOD conversation flow** (`CONVERSATION_FLOW=byod` in v1) | Azure OpenAI "On Your Data" delegation removed. Incompatible with Hard Rule #7 (no direct `openai`/`AzureOpenAI` SDK in v2; On Your Data is invoked via that SDK's `data_sources` parameter, which Foundry IQ does not expose as a drop-in), Hard Rule #5 (orchestrator-uniform interface; BYOD collapses the pipeline into one server-side call with no LangGraph / Agent Framework nodes), Hard Rule #6 (typed SSE reasoning channel; BYOD produces no per-token reasoning deltas), and Hard Rule #4 (registry plug-and-play; BYOD is Cosmos-AI-Search-only and forbids the pgvector provider). v2 ships the Custom flow only — app-owned retrieve → prompt → answer via Foundry IQ + registry orchestrators. **No code was ever written in v2 for BYOD**; this row makes the absence explicit. Drift note: [v2/docs/plan/business-cases.md](plan/business-cases.md) previously listed BYOD as "Kept" — corrected in the same turn (2026-05-20). **Clarifier (2026-06-09, Phase 8 / ADR 0021 — this does *not* re-introduce BYOD):** what is removed is specifically the Azure OpenAI `data_sources` ("On Your Data") **mechanism** — not platform-grounded retrieval as an *intent*. That intent returns through the compliant, registry-dispatched `agent_framework` orchestrator + Foundry IQ Knowledge Base (a `searchIndex` knowledge source wrapping the existing `cwyd-index`, queried live so continuous push-ingestion needs no reseed). That path satisfies the four rules BYOD broke: it runs on the Foundry **agent runtime** (not the `openai` SDK `data_sources` call) → #7; it is a uniform `OrchestratorBase` impl → #5; it emits the typed SSE reasoning channel → #6; and orchestrator selection stays registry-dispatched, with `pgvector` deployments required to use `langgraph` — selecting `agent_framework` in pgvector mode raises a clean, reusable `ConfigResolutionError` (HTTP 409 + ERROR telemetry) per ADR 0022, never a silent fallback (Foundry IQ has no pgvector knowledge source) → #4. See §4 Phase 8 for the ordered task table. |

### 2.2 Additions

| Component | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| **Azure AI Agent Framework** | Modern agent orchestration — replaces Semantic Kernel and Prompt Flow |
| **Foundry IQ** (Knowledge Base, Embeddings, Models) | Centralized knowledge base, embeddings, and model access (GPT-\*, o-series reasoning) — sole inference + retrieval surface |
| **LangGraph orchestrator** | Replaces v1's `ZeroShotAgent` / `AgentExecutor` LangChain pattern |

### 2.3 Updates

| Component | From → To |
|-----------|-----------|
| **Web framework** | Flask → **FastAPI** (async-native, OpenAPI docs, dependency injection, lifespan-managed singletons) |
| **Configuration** | `EnvHelper` singleton → **Pydantic `BaseSettings`** (typed, validated, nested) + DB-backed `RuntimeConfig` for live tweaks |
| **Project structure** | Monolithic `code/` → **modular `v2/src/`** (`backend/`, `backend/core/`, `frontend/`, `functions/`, `functions/core/`) — Phase 5.5 refactor |
| **Admin UI** | Standalone Streamlit app → **merged into React/Vite frontend** (Phase 5) |
| **Bicep infrastructure** | AVM-first; UAMI + RBAC; no Key Vault for app secrets; no one-click ARM |
| **Static type checking** | None → **`pyright --strict`** as a hard CI gate (`include = src/backend, src/functions`; `strict = src/backend/**, src/functions/core/**` post-refactor) |

### 2.4 Empty `__init__.py` invariant (locked 2026-05-20)

This section is the **single source of truth** for Hard Rule #13 in [.github/copilot-instructions.md](../../.github/copilot-instructions.md). The rule itself is intentionally short; the rationale, violation taxonomy, and migration plan live here.

#### 2.4.1 The rule (binding)

Every `v2/**/__init__.py` contains **at most one element**: the module docstring (including the `Pillar:` / `Phase:` header where applicable). Anything else is a violation.

#### 2.4.2 Why (project-goal alignment)

This project's core principles — *clean, modular, plug-and-play, no over-engineering* (Hard Rule #9) — are routinely undermined by code in `__init__.py`. Three concrete failure modes we've hit:

1. **Hidden import-time side effects.** Decorator-based registration via `from . import concrete_a` inside `__init__.py` means `import backend.core.providers.parsers` silently instantiates a `Registry`, imports every concrete, and fires every `@register` decorator. A reader who greps for `"pdf"` finds the registration but not the trigger. Moving these to a *named* sibling (`registry.py`) doesn't eliminate the side effect, but it makes the file's name match its behavior — "this module holds the registry" is honest; "this folder is a package" is not.
2. **Zero-value indirection (`create(key, **kwargs)`).** The seven provider domains each defined `def create(key, **kwargs): return registry.get(key)(**kwargs)`. The wrapper added no validation, no defaulting, no logging — a pure rename that disguised a dict lookup as factory logic. Callers `parsers.create("pdf")` look up the same `registry.get`-then-instantiate path; the function existed only because it was traditional.
3. **Mixed-purpose `__init__.py`.** Once one `def` is allowed, the file accretes helpers, constants, and re-exports. The strict invariant ("only a docstring") is enforceable by a 15-line AST test; "keep it light" is judgment-based and rots.

The rule serves the four principles directly:
- *Clean*: package boundaries are declarative — a folder is a folder, not a hidden module.
- *Modular*: every concrete is traceable to its registration in exactly one named file (`<domain>/registry.py`).
- *Plug-and-play*: callers can swap implementations without `__init__.py`-side magic.
- *No over-engineering*: `create()` wrappers, `__all__` lists, and re-export curation are all removed because none of them paid for themselves.

#### 2.4.3 Violation taxonomy

| # | Construct in `__init__.py` | Status | Why |
|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | Module docstring (incl. `Pillar:` / `Phase:` header) | ✅ allowed (and required where the package has a pillar) | Only legal content. |
| 2 | `__future__` / `TYPE_CHECKING` imports | ❌ forbidden | Already banned by Hard Rule #11. |
| 3 | `from .submodule import Symbol` (re-export) | ❌ forbidden | Callers must reach the symbol explicitly via its real module. |
| 4 | `from . import submodule` (side-effect import) | ❌ forbidden | Belongs in `<domain>/registry.py` next to the registry it populates. |
| 5 | `__all__ = [...]` | ❌ forbidden | A consequence of #3; nothing to list once re-exports are gone. |
| 6 | `registry = Registry("<domain>")` (or any instantiation) | ❌ forbidden | Module-level state lives in a named file. |
| 7 | Module-level constants (`FOO = "bar"`) | ❌ forbidden | If ≥2 form a closed set use `StrEnum` (Hard Rule #11); single values live in the consumer module. |
| 8 | `def helper(...)` / `class X: ...` | ❌ forbidden | Code lives in a named file describing its purpose. |
| 9 | `def create(key, **kwargs)` factory wrappers | ❌ forbidden | Removed 2026-05-20 — callers do `registry.get(key)(**kwargs)` directly. |

Enforcement: `v2/tests/shared/test_init_files_are_marker_only.py` (added in IA-C1). AST walk over every `v2/**/__init__.py`; the only top-level node accepted is `ast.Expr(value=ast.Constant(value=str))`. Anything else — including a stray `pass`, an `import`, or an assignment — fails the test with the file path and offending node line.

#### 2.4.4 Where displaced code goes

| Displaced from `__init__.py` | New home |
|---|---|
| `Registry[...]` instance for a provider domain | `<domain>/registry.py` (this is the *canonical* name; the file *is* a registry) |
| Eager `from . import concrete_a, concrete_b` that trigger `@register` decorators | `<domain>/registry.py` after the `Registry(...)` instantiation (`# noqa: E402, F401` on the import line) |
| Genuine domain helper (e.g. `credentials.select_default(...)`) | `<domain>/registry.py` next to the registry it consults |
| Re-exported symbols from a non-provider package (e.g. `backend/core/agents/`) | Removed; callers import the real module (`backend.core.agents.definitions`) |
| Pillar / Phase header | Stays in the `__init__.py` docstring — documentation only, no runtime effect |

**Naming exception:** if a future package's primary content is genuinely not a registry, name the sibling for what it *is* (`definitions.py`, `contracts.py`, etc.) — never put it back in `__init__.py`.

#### 2.4.5 Caller pattern (one shape, no variants)

```python
# CORRECT — explicit submodule import, no sugar.
from backend.core.providers.credentials import registry as credentials_registry

provider = credentials_registry.registry.get(settings.credentials.kind)(settings=settings)
default = credentials_registry.select_default(settings)
```

Forbidden caller shapes:
- `from backend.core.providers.credentials import create` (no `create`).
- `from backend.core.providers.credentials import registry` (without `as <domain>_registry`) — ambiguous reads (`registry.registry.get(...)` chain is confusing).
- `import backend.core.providers.credentials as credentials; credentials.create(...)` (no module-level `create`).

#### 2.4.6 Audit baseline (2026-05-20)

24 `__init__.py` files under `v2/src/` and `v2/tests/`:

| Classification | Count | Action |
|---|---|---|
| Empty marker | 8 | ✅ no change |
| Docstring-only | 8 | ✅ no change |
| Re-export only (`backend/core/agents/__init__.py`) | 1 | ⏭ migrate per strict rule (callers import `backend.core.agents.definitions` directly) |
| **Has logic (Registry + `create()` + side-effect imports)** | **7** | ⏭ migrate to sibling `registry.py` |

The 7 violators (all under [v2/src/backend/core/providers/](../src/backend/core/providers)): `credentials`, `databases`, `llm`, `orchestrators`, `search`, `parsers`, `agents`.

#### 2.4.7 Migration sequence (1 unit per turn, smallest blast radius first)

| Unit | Domain | Callsites to update |
|---|---|---|
| IA-B1 | `parsers` | tests only (no app.py callers yet) |
| IA-B2 | `credentials` | 2 in [app.py](../src/backend/app.py) (incl. `select_default`) |
| IA-B3 | `llm` | 1 in app.py |
| IA-B4 | `agents` (provider) | 1 in app.py |
| IA-B5 | `databases` | 2 (app.py, [routers/health.py](../src/backend/routers/health.py)) |
| IA-B6 | `search` | 2 (app.py, health.py) + 2 test files |
| IA-B7 | `orchestrators` | 1 in [routers/conversation.py](../src/backend/routers/conversation.py) |
| IA-B8 | `backend/core/agents/` re-export migration | callers of `BUILTIN_AGENTS`, `CWYD_AGENT`, `RAI_AGENT`, `AgentDefinition` |
| IA-C1 | AST enforcement test | `v2/tests/shared/test_init_files_are_marker_only.py` |
| IA-D1 | Audit close | dev_plan §0.1 ledger row |

#### 2.4.8 Per-domain recipe

1. Create `<domain>/registry.py` holding (in order): the `Registry[...]` instance, eager side-effect imports of concretes, any genuine helper (`select_default` for credentials only).
2. Update every concrete in the domain: `from . import registry` → `from .registry import registry`.
3. Empty out `__init__.py` to a module-docstring-only marker (preserve `Pillar:` / `Phase:` header).
4. Update all callsites: `<domain>.create(key, **kwargs)` → `<domain>_registry.registry.get(key)(**kwargs)`; `<domain>.select_default(...)` → `<domain>_registry.select_default(...)` (where `<domain>_registry` is the alias from `from backend.core.providers.<domain> import registry as <domain>_registry`).
5. Run `pytest -q` + `pyright src/functions src/backend`; append ledger row.

The IA-Bx work is **not** part of any numeric §4 phase — it is a cross-cutting Hard-Rule-#13 cleanup that lands between Phase 6 units when the user explicitly schedules it (the Phase 6 ordered backlog in §4.6.1 stays the active queue otherwise).

---

## 3. v2 Target Architecture

### 3.1 High-level

```
                   ┌──────────────────────────────┐
                   │       USERS (Browser)         │
                   └───────────────┬──────────────┘
                                   │
                   ┌───────────────▼──────────────┐
                   │  React/Vite Frontend          │
                   │  Chat + Admin (unified)       │
                   │  Azure App Service            │
                   └───────────────┬──────────────┘
                                   │ REST / SSE
                   ┌───────────────▼──────────────┐
                   │  FastAPI Backend              │
                   │  Routers: conversation,       │
                   │           history, admin,     │
                   │           health              │
                   │  Azure Container App          │
                   └──┬──────────┬──────────────┬─┘
                      │          │              │
              ┌───────▼───┐  ┌───▼────┐  ┌──────▼────────┐
              │backend.   │  │backend.│  │  Foundry IQ   │
              │core.      │  │core.   │  │  (Knowledge,  │
              │orchestra- │  │data-   │  │   Embeddings, │
              │tors       │  │bases   │  │   Models)     │
              │ (langgraph│  │(cosmos │  │  ├─ GPT-*    │
              │  + agent_ │  │ + pg-  │  │  ├─ o-series │
              │  framework│  │ vector)│  │  └─ Embed.   │
              └───────────┘  └────────┘  └───────────────┘
```

### 3.2 RAG indexing pipeline (Phase 6 — split Azure Functions, **opt-in**)

Functions container only spins up when the operator wants user file uploads. Backend container runs chat end-to-end without it.

```
 ┌──────────────┐    ┌──────────────┐    ┌─────────────────┐
 │ Blob Storage │───▶│ Event Grid   │───▶│ Queue Storage   │
 │ (Documents)  │    │ (Trigger)    │    │ (Process Msgs)  │
 └──────────────┘    └──────────────┘    └────────┬────────┘
                                                  │
                  ┌───────────────────────────────▼────────────┐
                  │  Azure Functions (Modular)                  │
                  │  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐         │
                  │  │ batch_start  │  │ batch_push   │         │
                  │  │ (list+queue) │  │ (parse+chunk │         │
                  │  └──────────────┘  │  +embed+push)│         │
                  │  ┌──────────────┐  └──────────────┘         │
                  │  │ add_url      │  ┌──────────────┐         │
                  │  │ (URL fetch+  │  │ search_skill │         │
                  │  │  embed)      │  │ (custom AI   │         │
                  │  └──────────────┘  │  Search skill│         │
                  │                    └──────────────┘         │
                  │  Each blueprint lives in v2/src/functions/  │
                  │  Ingestion-only extensions in functions/core│
                  │  Imports backend.core for shared providers  │
                  └─────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### 3.3 Orchestrator migration (v1 → v2)

```
v1 Orchestrators                     v2 Orchestrators
───────────────────                  ─────────────────────────
OpenAI Functions     ──────────▶     (Removed; Agent Framework + Foundry replaces)
Semantic Kernel      ─────╳────▶     REMOVED
LangChain Agent      ──────────▶     LangGraph (StateGraph + ToolNode)
Prompt Flow          ─────╳────▶     REMOVED
                                     Agent Framework (NEW; via Foundry agents)

Model Access:
v1: Direct Azure OpenAI SDK   ──▶   v2: Foundry IQ
                                         ├── GPT-* (chat)
                                         ├── o-series (reasoning)
                                         └── text-embedding-3-* (embed)
```

### 3.4 File-level inventory

> Phase 5.5 closed 2026-05-06: `v2/src/shared/**` was `git mv`'d to `v2/src/backend/core/**` and `v2/src/functions/core/` exists as the empty extension skeleton (populated in Phase 6). The tree below is the **current** on-disk state.

```
v2/
├── azure.yaml                          # azd service definitions
├── pyproject.toml                      # mono-package (backend + functions)
├── Makefile                            # typecheck / test / lint targets
├── docker/
│   ├── docker-compose.dev.yml          # backend-only + frontend-only profiles
│   ├── Dockerfile.backend
│   ├── Dockerfile.frontend
│   ├── Dockerfile.functions            # copies src/backend (for backend.core) + src/functions
│   └── ci-entrypoint.sh
├── docs/
│   ├── development_plan.md             # this file (canonical)
│   ├── development_plan.old.md         # historical ledger (frozen 2026-05-06)
│   ├── pillars_of_development.md       # read-only product policy
│   ├── exception_handling_policy.md    # NEW in Phase 5.5 (Phase C)
│   ├── env-vars.md
│   ├── agents.md
│   └── adr/
│       ├── 0001..0008-*.md             # accepted ADRs
│       └── 0009-runtime-type-imports.md (only if Phase B needed leaf-extraction)
├── infra/                              # Bicep AVM-first
│   ├── main.bicep
│   └── modules/...
├── scripts/
│   ├── post_provision.{sh,ps1}
│   └── post_provision.py
├── src/
│   ├── backend/
│   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   ├── app.py                      # FastAPI app + lifespan
│   │   ├── dependencies.py             # DI seams
│   │   ├── core/                       # ← shared/ moved here in Phase B
│   │   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   │   ├── registry.py
│   │   │   ├── settings.py             # Pydantic BaseSettings + AppSettings
│   │   │   ├── types.py                # OrchestratorEvent + RuntimeConfig + StrEnums
│   │   │   ├── agents/
│   │   │   │   ├── __init__.py
│   │   │   │   └── definitions.py      # CWYD_AGENT, RAI_AGENT, BUILTIN_AGENTS
│   │   │   ├── providers/
│   │   │   │   ├── credentials/        # cli, managed_identity
│   │   │   │   ├── llm/                # foundry_iq + BaseLLMProvider.complete()
│   │   │   │   ├── search/             # azure_search, pgvector
│   │   │   │   ├── databases/          # cosmosdb, postgres
│   │   │   │   ├── agents/             # foundry (lazy DB-backed bootstrap)
│   │   │   │   └── orchestrators/      # langgraph, agent_framework
│   │   │   ├── pipelines/
│   │   │   │   └── chat.py             # run_chat() — content-safety + RAI gates + orchestrator iteration
│   │   │   └── tools/                  # content_safety, post_prompt, qa, text_processing, citations
│   │   ├── models/                     # Pydantic request/response
│   │   │   ├── conversation.py
│   │   │   └── health.py
│   │   └── routers/
│   │       ├── conversation.py         # POST /api/conversation (SSE)
│   │       ├── history.py              # /api/history/*
│   │       ├── health.py               # /api/health, /api/health/ready
│   │       └── admin.py                # /api/admin/config (GET + PATCH)
│   ├── frontend/                       # React 19 + Vite + TS (no UI library)
│   │   ├── src/
│   │   ├── frontend_app.py             # tiny FastAPI + StaticFiles prod shim
│   │   └── package.json
│   └── functions/
│       ├── __init__.py
│       ├── function_app.py             # currently a stub; blueprints land in Phase 6
│       ├── host.json
│       └── core/                       # ← created empty in Phase B; populated in Phase 6
│           └── __init__.py             # ingestion-only extensions; imports backend.core
└── tests/
    ├── backend/
    │   ├── core/                       # ← tests/shared/ moved here in Phase B
    │   ├── test_app_lifespan.py
    │   ├── test_admin.py
    │   ├── test_conversation.py
    │   ├── test_history.py
    │   └── test_health.py
    ├── frontend/
    ├── functions/
    │   └── core/                       # mirror of src/functions/core/
    ├── infra/
    │   └── test_main_bicep.py
    └── shared/                         # AST invariant tests (cross-cutting)
        └── test_no_type_checking_or_future_annotations.py
```

**The four "what lives where" rules** (locked in for Phase 5.5):

| Rule | Destination |
|---|---|
| Used **only** by backend at chat/query time | `v2/src/backend/core/` |
| Used **only** by functions for indexing/RAG ingestion | `v2/src/functions/core/` |
| Used by **both** backend and functions | `v2/src/backend/core/` (functions imports from it) |
| Used **only** by functions but extends a `backend.core` library | `v2/src/functions/core/` (subclass / extension module that imports the base from `backend.core`) |

**Anti-duplication invariant**: no symbol is defined twice. If functions needs to add behavior to a `backend.core` provider (e.g., a chunking strategy on a parser), the subclass lives in `functions.core` and inherits from `backend.core`. Enforced by code review — no automated check today.

## 4. Phases

### Phase 5 (backend closed 2026-05-07) — Admin + Frontend Merge

Backend surface (#35a–#35c, #35e, #35f, #39) all ✅ done. **Open items
that do NOT block Phase 6:** #35d is FE-team owned (React admin
routes) and tracked separately; #35g (per-tenant overrides) is
**withdrawn as out of scope** — the single-tenant deployment makes
tenant-keyed config a functional no-op over the singleton (see
[ADR 0024](adr/0024-withdraw-per-tenant-runtime-config-single-tenant.md),
which supersedes ADR 0023). Phase 6
(Functions blueprints — modular RAG indexing pipeline) is unblocked.

| # | Task | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| 35a | `GET /api/admin/config` | ✅ done | 6-field shape: orchestrator key, OpenAI temperature/max_tokens, search semantic-toggle/top_k, log_level. |
| 35b | `RuntimeConfig` model + `CosmosItemType.CONFIG` enum | ✅ done | Cosmos `_system` partition (mirrors CU-010b1 `AGENT` precedent); Postgres `runtime_config` single-row JSONB table. |
| 35c | `PATCH /api/admin/config` (DB-backed, RFC 7396 merge) | ✅ done | `get_runtime_config` + `upsert_runtime_config` on `BaseDatabaseClient` + Cosmos + Postgres impls; PATCH route with `_WRITABLE_FIELDS` frozenset; explicit `null` reverts to env default. |
| 35d | Frontend admin merge | ✅ done (2026-06-08) | Configuration form + document upload + prompt editor shipped as React admin pages (closure trail `U-P7-35D-AUDIT` across `U-P7-PROMPT-1..4` + `U-P7-CFG-1..3`; see §0.1). Browser-URL routing for these pages is a separate post-Phase-7 enhancement — see §0.0c `U-PP7-ROUTE`. |

[ADR 0023](adr/0023-per-tenant-runtime-config-keying.md) **superseded by [ADR 0024](adr/0024-withdraw-per-tenant-runtime-config-single-tenant.md)**; the speculative tenant-claim seam (`get_tenant_id` + `TenantIdDep` + `_extract_tenant_id` + 9 tests) is removed. Singleton `RuntimeConfig` + the `#35e(a)` cache retained. Reopen only if multi-org becomes real. |
| 39 | Admin RBAC narrowing | ✅ done (2026-05-06) | `requires_role("admin")` dependency on all `/api/admin/*` routes; details in §0.1. |

### Phase 6 — RAG Indexing Pipeline (Split Functions)

Land the four blueprints under `v2/src/functions/`:

| # | Blueprint | Trigger | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| 40 | `batch_start` | HTTP / Timer | List blobs, fan-out to queue. |
| 41 | `batch_push` | Queue (Storage) | Parse → chunk → embed → push to search index. Uses parser/chunker from `functions.core` (extensions of `backend.core` parsers). |
| 42 | `add_url` | HTTP | Fetch URL content, parse, embed. |
| 43 | `search_skill` | HTTP (custom AI Search skill endpoint) | Sync embed-on-the-fly used by AI Search indexer. |

Each blueprint ships with the per-trigger try/except pattern from Phase 5.5 §C1 policy doc. Poison queue handling per Functions retry policy.

**Phase 6 also lands**: standalone-backend smoke test (CI job that boots `docker compose --profile backend-only up` and runs `/api/conversation` against a mocked OpenAI to prove the "backend works without functions" claim).

#### 4.6.1 Phase 6 ordered unit backlog

**Deterministic Hard-Rule-#1 sequence. The agent picks the next ☐ row without prompting the user.** Locked 2026-05-20 after U8b. Per-unit contract auto-applies (one class OR one method, ≥3 tests, narrow SDK exception catch + `logger.exception` + re-raise, pillar header docstring, pytest new → pytest full → pyright `src/functions src/backend` → §0.1 ledger row → end-of-turn beep).

| U11.5 | ✅ | Comment-scrub policy: codify Hard Rule #16, sweep `v2/src/**`, ship AST gate | `.github/copilot-instructions.md`, `tests/shared/test_no_process_narrative_in_src.py`, scrub of `functions/{function_app,batch_push,batch_start,add_url,search_skill}/*.py` + `functions/core/{__init__,contracts,exception_mapping,storage_clients,storage_endpoints,http,parsers/text_parser}.py` + `backend/core/{types,settings,providers/llm/{base,foundry_iq},providers/orchestrators/{agent_framework,langgraph}}.py` | U11 |
| U12 | ✅ | Phase 6 close audit (flip Phase 6 ⏳→✅, bump Phase 7 ⏭) | dev_plan only | U11.5 |

**Locked decisions (no future "which path" prompts):**

- **D1** `BaseParser` and `BaseEmbedder` ABCs live in `backend/core/providers/` (Stable Core) per registry-first Hard Rule #4. Ingestion-only concretes (PDF/DOCX) live in `functions/core/parsers/` as backend-base extensions.
- **D2** No standalone `Chunker` primitive — parsers return `list[Chunk]` directly (matches v1 `embed_file` flow; one registry tier).
- **D3** Only `TextParser` ships in U8d. PDF/DOCX/MD parsers go in §0.1 as deferred items, added in Phase 7 unless a demo blocks.
- **D4** Search write-side is a **helper function** (`push_documents`), not a new `SearchWriter` registry. Existing `providers/search/` is read-side; write is one-shot.
- **D5** `function_app.py` registration is sequential — no Functions-app registry (mounting, not provider dispatch).
- **D6** `Chunk` value type lives in `backend/core/types.py` (not coupled to parser module) — same convention as `OrchestratorChannel`. Frozen, hashable, Pydantic `BaseModel` with `extra="forbid"`.

**Structural sign-off (Hard Rule #10, granted 2026-05-20 with "Start implementation"):**
1. New package `backend/core/providers/parsers/` ✅ approved
2. New package `backend/core/providers/embedders/` ✅ approved
3. New file `backend/core/providers/search/writer.py` ✅ approved
4. New packages `functions/core/parsers/`, `functions/add_url/`, `functions/search_skill/` ✅ approved

All four are anticipated by [v2/src/backend/core/providers/__init__.py](../src/backend/core/providers/__init__.py) module docstring — this fills declared scaffolding, no surprise structure.

- End-to-end Playwright tests against the deployed environment (`v2/tests/e2e/`).
- Coverage report gate (`uv run pytest --cov=src/backend --cov-fail-under=80`).
- Operator runbook expansion in `v2/docs/`.
- ADR backfill for any Phase 5.5 / Phase 6 architectural decisions not already captured.

Sequencing is TBD at the Phase 7 opening turn — the rolling Phase 7 bullets above interleave with these task rows.
