| # | Source | Scope | Files | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 50 | T1-17 + T3-4 | Feedback thumbs (👍 / 👎 + reason picker) on assistant messages | `v2/src/frontend/src/pages/chat/components/{MessageList,FeedbackButtons}.{tsx,module.css}`, `v2/src/frontend/src/api/feedback.ts`, `v2/src/frontend/tests/**` | Backend wired in #32b (`/api/history/messages/{id}/feedback`); FE work only. |
| 51 | T6-1 | PDF parser registered as `ingestion_parsers_registry["pdf"]` via **Azure Document Intelligence** on the unified Foundry AI Services endpoint (`azure-ai-documentintelligence>=1.0` SDK, UAMI auth) | `v2/src/functions/core/parsers/pdf_parser.py` (new), `v2/src/functions/core/parsers/registry.py` (eager import), `v2/tests/functions/core/parsers/test_pdf_parser.py` (new), `DocumentIntelligenceSettings` (already landed in U-P7-B0) | v2-native shape — parser calls Document Intelligence at `{foundry.services_endpoint}documentintelligence/...` via the modern `azure-ai-documentintelligence>=1.0` SDK pointed at the unified AI Services account (`kind=AIServices`, `allowProjectManagement=true`) declared in `v2/infra/main.bicep`. Legacy `azure-ai-formrecognizer>=3.3,<4.0` dep swapped out in U-P7-B0 so Unit B only adds the parser class + registry wiring. |
| 52 | T6-2 | DOCX parser registered as `ingestion_parsers_registry["docx"]` on the shared `DocumentIntelligenceParser` class (same `prebuilt-layout` model as PDF #51 — no new parser file) | `v2/src/functions/core/parsers/document_intelligence_parser.py` (add second `@registry.register("docx")` decorator above the existing `@registry.register("pdf")`; rename from `pdf_parser.py` lands in this same unit), `v2/src/functions/core/parsers/registry.py` (point the eager-import line at the renamed module), `v2/tests/functions/core/parsers/test_document_intelligence_parser.py` (renamed from `test_pdf_parser.py`; extend the two registration tests with a `("pdf", "docx")` parametrise) | **Ships as a one-decorator extension of the class delivered in Unit B / U-P7-51 — no new code surface, no new SDK call, no new credential, no new RBAC.** `prebuilt-layout` natively supports PDF + DOCX + XLSX + PPTX + HTML + images on the same `begin_analyze_document` call, so adding a `DocxParser` clone would be ~90% duplicate code and would cement a one-class-per-extension precedent that scales linearly with formats. T6-3 (MD/HTML) and T6-5 (image parsers) can land the same way with one decorator each if/when their DEFER-PHASE-8 gates open. **Class rename `PdfParser` → `DocumentIntelligenceParser` is folded into this unit** (Hard Rule #11 carve-out: rename is safe while the symbol has only one-turn-old eager-import registration and zero external consumers; doing it later, after a 3rd or 4th format ships against the same model, would be materially more expensive). |
| 53 | T2-1 | Ingest Data admin UI: file upload + URL form + **reprocess-all** button (full v1 scope) | `v2/src/frontend/src/pages/admin/IngestData/**` (new page), `v2/src/frontend/src/api/admin.ts` (extend), tests | Full v1 scope per user pick — reprocess-all is an operator requirement at customer scale. Wires `POST /api/admin/documents{,/url,/reprocess}` (FastAPI route handlers in `routers/admin.py`; service helpers in `services/ingestion.py`); single-ingress to FastAPI is the v2 canonical pattern (user direction 2026-06-02; Functions HTTP triggers stay internal plumbing). **Closed via U-P7-53-BE (3 backend units 2026-06-02) + U-P7-53-FE (3 frontend units 2026-06-02..2026-06-03) + U-P7-53-AUDIT (2026-06-03).** |
| 54 | T2-3 | Delete Data admin UI: multi-select delete from index + blob | `v2/src/frontend/src/pages/admin/DeleteData/**` (new page), backend `DELETE /api/admin/documents/{id}` (new), tests | Full v1 scope per user pick. GDPR + customer-deletion = real ask. **Progress:** backend route + search-provider delete contract are shipped; FE multi-select delete + selected-failed retry are shipped. **Remaining:** final parity closure + operator-flow UX acceptance. |
| ⇢ #35d | T2-4 | Configuration UI (already open in §0.1) — operator-facing admin page consuming `/api/admin/config/*` | (see §0.1 #35d) | Cross-reference; no duplication. |
| ⇢ #24 | T3-1 | Citation panel (already partial in §0.2) — `<CitationPanel>` collapsible accordion + clickable `[docN]` rich-text tokens | (see §0.2 #24) | Cross-reference; no duplication. |

**Explicitly out of Phase 7 scope** (DEFER-PHASE-8 from parity audit): T2-2 Explore Data UI, T3-2 TTS speaker button, T3-3 share URL, T6-3 MD/HTML parser, T6-4 JSON parser, T6-5 image parsers. **9 items rejected as v1-spaghetti** per the validity test: T1-1, T1-2, T1-3, T1-4, T1-6, T1-13, T1-14, T1-18, T3-5. Full classification trail in [v1_v2_parity_decisions.md](v1_v2_parity_decisions.md).

**Sequencing rule (Hard Rule #1).** Each task above lands as one or more single-unit turns at the implementation step. Cross-reference rows do not add new work — they re-surface existing §0.1 / §0.2 items so the Phase 7 surface is complete in one place.

---

### Phase 8 — `agent_framework` default + Foundry IQ Knowledge Base retrieval

Makes `agent_framework` the default orchestrator, grounded by a Foundry IQ Knowledge Base (the rules-compliant successor to the v1 BYOD *intent* — see §2.1 clarifier; **not** the removed `data_sources` mechanism). Opened by §0.0d (2026-06-09). Ratified in [ADR 0021](adr/0021-agent-framework-foundry-iq-kb-default.md) (Proposed → Accepted at task `C`) + [ADR 0022](adr/0022-config-resolution-error-on-incompatible-overrides.md) (Proposed → Accepted at task `B5b`). Pillar split: **Configuration Layer** (settings + default selection + env-pinned API version) over a **Stable Core** seam (KB tool binding on the existing `agent_framework` orchestrator + the index_store→orchestrator guardrail).

**Invariants for this phase.** (a) One unit + test per turn (Hard Rule #1/#2). (b) The default flip (task `C`) lands **last**, only after KB retrieval is wired and verified — never ship an ungrounded default. (c) The KB API version is a plain `str` settings field (externally pinned, follows `AZURE_*_API_VERSION`); any new closed-set string literal uses `StrEnum` (Hard Rule #11). (d) Every turn ends with the relevant `uv run pytest -q` subset + `uv run pyright src/backend src/functions` green and all AST gates green. (e) No new top-level folder / package / module layout — all edits extend existing files (Hard Rule #10); the two new ADRs live in the existing `v2/docs/adr/`.

**Ordered task table** (the canonical resumable checklist — execute top-to-bottom; each row is one or more single-unit turns; strictly linear `B0 → B1 → B-Spike → B2 → B3 → B4 → B5a → B5b → C`):

| # | Task | Kind | Files | Test / gate |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| B0 | Guidance-sync: §2.1 BYOD clarifier + §0.0d receipt + this Phase 8 block + ADRs 0021/0022 (Proposed) + ADR index completion + project_status Phase 8 note | doc only | `v2/docs/development_plan.md`, `v2/docs/adr/{0021,0022}-*.md`, `v2/docs/adr/README.md`, `v2/docs/project_status.md` | n/a (doc) — **this row; landed 2026-06-09** |
| B1 | `SearchSettings` gains `knowledge_base_name="cwyd-kb"`, `knowledge_source_name="cwyd-index-ks"`, `knowledge_base_api_version="2025-11-01-preview"` (env `AZURE_AI_SEARCH_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_API_VERSION`); document in `.env.sample` | code + test | `v2/src/backend/core/settings.py`, `v2/.env.sample` | settings test: env override beats the `2025-11-01-preview` default + defaults present |
| B-Spike | Confirm the pinned `azure-ai-projects` / `agent-framework` surface (`MCPTool` + `PromptAgentDefinition` + `create_version` vs current `AgentsClient.create_agent`; `FoundryChatClient`; `OpenAIChatOptions`). Pick KB consume path **A** (agent-side `MCPTool` → managed KB MCP endpoint) vs **B** (app-side KB retrieve via Search SDK). Verify `cwyd-index` named semantic config (`default` ✅) + whether a default scoring profile is required. Resolves the ADR 0021 open questions. **Resolved 2026-06-09 (see [ADR 0021](adr/0021-agent-framework-foundry-iq-kb-default.md) “Spike findings”): consume path A2 (`agent_framework.MCPStreamableHTTPTool` on the current `FoundryAgent`, bound via `run(tools=[...])`); no scoring profile needed; KB seeded via Search REST `knowledgesources`/`knowledgebases` (no SDK model class); knobs via `FoundryAgent default_options`, not `OpenAIChatOptions` (absent from the 1.7.0 pin).** | research (read-only) | (no code) — updates [ADR 0021](adr/0021-agent-framework-foundry-iq-kb-default.md) open-questions | n/a (research) — **landed 2026-06-09**; output gates B2 + B4 |
| B2 | `post_provision.py`: one-time create `searchIndex` knowledge source over `cwyd-index` + the KB (reasoning model); reads the API version from settings. Idempotent (create-or-update); **not** per-document | code + test | `v2/scripts/post_provision.py` | seed-builder shape + idempotency (create-vs-update) test |
| B3 | Bicep: per-KB project connection so the agent resolves the KB by name (extend `ai-project-search-connection.bicep` or a sibling module) | infra + test | `v2/infra/modules/**`, `v2/infra/main.bicep` | `bicep build` clean + param/output wiring assertion |
| B4 | Bind the KB tool (consume path **A2**: `agent_framework.MCPStreamableHTTPTool` → managed KB MCP endpoint) into `AgentFrameworkOrchestrator` via `FoundryAgent.run(tools=[...])`; thread `temperature` / `max_tokens` via the `FoundryAgent` `default_options` / run `options` (the pin has **no** `OpenAIChatOptions`; no `top_k`); likely drop the bare `"search"` placeholder from `CWYD_AGENT.tools` | code + test | `v2/src/backend/core/providers/orchestrators/agent_framework.py` | agent built with KB tool; knobs forwarded; reasoning channel still emitted |
| B5a | `ConfigResolutionError` reusable domain exception (first custom backend exception, Stable Core) + `app.py` app-level handler → HTTP 409 + ERROR-level structured telemetry log | code + test | `v2/src/backend/services/admin.py`, `v2/src/backend/app.py` | raise → 409 JSON body; exactly one ERROR log with structured `extra`; handler registered alongside the existing five |
| B5b | Encode the pgvector + `agent_framework` rule in `resolve_effective_config` (raise `ConfigResolutionError(reason="orchestrator_requires_azure_search")`); document the operator fix (`CWYD_ORCHESTRATOR_NAME=langgraph` for pgvector) in env / runbook docs. Move **ADR 0022 → Accepted** | code + test + docs | `v2/src/backend/services/admin.py`, `v2/.env.sample`, [ADR 0022](adr/0022-config-resolution-error-on-incompatible-overrides.md) | pg + agent_framework → raises 409; azure + agent_framework → ok; pg + langgraph → ok |
| C | Flip `OrchestratorSettings.name` default `"langgraph"` → `"agent_framework"`. Move **ADR 0021 → Accepted**. Update `project_status.md` (Executive Status + BYOD-row cross-ref + orchestrator row + re-baseline metrics) | code + test + docs | `v2/src/backend/core/settings.py`, [ADR 0021](adr/0021-agent-framework-foundry-iq-kb-default.md), `v2/docs/project_status.md` | default-selection test + existing orchestrator tests green; **only after B5 green** — **landed 2026-06-09** |

**Dependencies.** `B-Spike` gates `B2` + `B4` (the consume-path decision shapes their code). `B3` (infra) may run in parallel with `B2` once the consume path is chosen. `B5b` depends on `B5a` (the exception + handler must exist before the resolver rule raises it). Task `C` (default flip) runs **only after `B5b` is green** — the pgvector guard must be enforced before `agent_framework` becomes the default.

**Decisions** (from the 2026-06-09 planning turns; change on request): pgvector guardrail = a clean, reusable `ConfigResolutionError` (HTTP 409 + ERROR-level telemetry) raised from `resolve_effective_config` — **not** a silent `langgraph` fallback, not a per-deployment doc note, not a pgvector function-tool (ADR 0022, repo-owner directive 2026-06-09); BYOD framing = the orchestrator selector *is* the v2 conversation-flow selector (`agent_framework` = compliant BYOD-intent successor, not `data_sources` revival).

**Out of Phase 8 scope.** The deferred parser shelf (T6-3 MD/HTML, T6-4 JSON, T6-5 images) and the multi-agent demo track (`B-IMPL-EXTRAS`) remain separate, independently-scoped work.

---

## 5. Pillars

See [pillars_of_development.md](pillars_of_development.md) — read-only product policy. Every new module/class in `v2/src/**` opens with:

```
Pillar: <Stable Core | Scenario Pack | Configuration Layer | Customization Layer>
Phase: <1..7 from this development_plan.md>
```

Agents reference the pillars file but never edit it. Any proposed change to pillars must be raised with the user as a separate request.

---

## 6. Naming conventions

Pointer to [.github/copilot-instructions.md](../../.github/copilot-instructions.md) Hard Rule #11. Highlights:

- **Python**: `snake_case` functions/methods/vars/modules, `PascalCase` classes, `UPPER_SNAKE_CASE` constants, `_leading_underscore` private. Closed-set string literals → `enum.StrEnum` (Python 3.11+), not module constants.
- **TypeScript**: `camelCase` vars/functions, `PascalCase` types/interfaces/components, `UPPER_SNAKE_CASE` constants, no `I`-prefix on interfaces.
- **Bicep**: `camelCase` for params/vars/modules/resources/outputs.
- **Cross-cutting**: env vars `UPPER_SNAKE_CASE` with prefixes (`AZURE_*`, `VITE_*`, `CWYD_*`); Azure resource names `<type-abbrev>-<solutionSuffix>` per `v2/infra/abbreviations.json`.
- **Public API names** (HTTP routes, OpenAPI operationIds, SSE event types, `OrchestratorEvent` fields) require user confirmation to rename once shipped.

---

## 7. Local development

Pointers to operational tooling:

- **Editable install**: `uv sync` from repo root.
- **Backend-only profile** (Phase 5.5 invariant: chat works without functions): `docker compose -f v2/docker/docker-compose.dev.yml --profile backend-only up`.
- **Frontend-only profile** (`VITE_BACKEND_URL` required): `docker compose -f v2/docker/docker-compose.dev.yml --profile frontend-only up`.
- **Full dev stack**: `docker compose -f v2/docker/docker-compose.dev.yml up`.
- **CI validation image**: `docker build -f v2/docker/Dockerfile.ci-validate -t cwyd-ci .` then run.
- **Type-check gate**: `uv run pyright` (CI hard-gate via `.github/workflows/v2-typecheck.yml` since Q14e closed 2026-05-06).
- **Test gate**: `uv run pytest` (547/547 baseline at start of Phase 5.5).
- **Provision-then-deploy**: `azd up` (one-shot) or `azd provision` → `azd deploy` (split).
